60:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":["Classical Lyapunov stability applies to unperturbed systems. In practice — and especially\nin sim-to-real — the robot always faces disturbances: model mismatch, sensor noise, terrain\nvariation. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Input-to-state stability (ISS)"}]," extends Lyapunov theory to perturbed systems:\na system is ISS if bounded disturbances produce bounded state deviations, with the bound\nscaling continuously from zero. 62:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":"Classical controllers come with stability guarantees derived from Lyapunov theory. Learned\ncontrollers generally do not — a policy that achieves high reward in training may be\nunstable in the Lyapunov sense and fail catastrophically under small perturbations at\ndeployment. c9:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":[["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"PID and joint-space PD control"}]," are the lowest layer of almost every real robot,\nincluding the action interface through which learned policies execute. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Stability and\nLyapunov theory"}]," provide the mathematical framework for certifying that controllers\nwork — and motivate CLFs, CBFs, and neural Lyapunov functions as tools for extending\nthose guarantees to learned systems. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Impedance control"}]," is the standard paradigm for\ncontact-rich manipulation and the substrate on which most imitation learning for assembly\nis built. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Task-space and operational-space control"}]," generalize joint-space control to\nCartesian objectives, and are the execution layer for manipulation policies that reason\nabout end-effector pose. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"LQR"}]," is optimal control in closed form — and the Riccati\nequation is the Bellman equation under linearity and quadratic cost, directly linking\ncontrol theory and ",["$","$L30",null,{"term":"RL"}],". ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"iLQR and DDP"}]," extend optimality to nonlinear systems through\niterative linearization, at the cost of assuming smooth dynamics. ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"MPC"}]," closes the\nloop by resolving the optimization online, giving robustness through feedback.\n",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"MPPI"}]," removes the smoothness assumption through sampling, bridging MPC and\ngradient-free ",["$","$L30",null,{"term":"RL"}],". And ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"hybrid architectures"}]," — residual policies and policy + controller\nstacks — are how these classical and learned components are combined in systems that\nactually deploy."]}]

1ba:["$","li",null,{"style":{"marginBottom":"0.35em","fontSize":"1rem"},"children":[["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Stiff position control for peg insertion."}]," A stiff controller commands exact positions, so tiny pose errors generate large contact forces and the peg wedges against the hole edge with no way to comply — jamming or excessive force.
